\"* Linear Regression Model for training and predictions\"","   ]","  },","  {","   \"cell_type\": \"code\",","   \"execution_count\": 19,","   \"metadata\": {},","   \"outputs\": [],","   \"source\": \"numerical_features\"","   ]","  },","  {","   \"cell_type\": \"markdown\",","   \"metadata\": {},","   \"source\": [","    \"### Custom Transformer\\n\",","    \"\\n\",","    \"Out-of-the-box sklearn one hot encoders do not support dropping one of the columns after hot encoding, and it also creates a problem while trying to retrieve the new column set post hot encoding when there are other transformations happening. Hence this option\"","   ]","  },","  {","   \"cell_type\": \"code\",","   \"execution_count\": 22,","   \"metadata\": {},","   \"outputs\": [],","   \"source\": [","    \"from sklearn.base import BaseEstimator, TransformerMixin\\n\",","    \"import pandas as pd\\n\",","    \"\\n\",","    \"class CustomOneHotEncoder(BaseEstimator, TransformerMixin):\\n\",","    \"    def __init__(self, categorical_features=None, reindex_columns=None):\\n\",","    \"        self.categorical_features = categorical_features\\n\",","    \"        self.reindex_columns = reindex_columns\\n\",","    \"        self.updated_feature_names = None\\n\",","    \"    \\n\",","    \"    def transform(self, X, **transformparams):\\n\",","    \"        #print (transformparams.get('arg1'))\\n\",","    \"        self.updated_feature_names = []\\n\",","    \"        hot_encoded_df = pd.get_dummies(data=X, columns=self.categorical_features, \\\\\\n\",","    \"                                        drop_first=False).copy()\\n\",","    \"        # Lets reindex this thing, which will add any missing columns in the passed data\\n\",","    \"        print(hot_encoded_df.shape)\\n\",","    \"        hot_encoded_df = hot_encoded_df.reindex(columns=self.reindex_columns, fill_value=0)\\n\",","    \"        print(hot_encoded_df.shape)\\n\",","    \"        # Now we have reformed the encoded dataframe by filling any missing columns\\n\",","    \"        self.updated_feature_names = hot_encoded_df.columns\\n\",","    \"        return hot_encoded_df\\n\",","    \"    \\n\",","    \"    def fit(self, X, y=None, **fitparams):\\n\",","    \"        return self\\n\",","    \"    \\n\",","    \"    def get_feature_names(self):\\n\",","    \"        return self.updated_feature_names\"","   ]","  },","  {","   \"cell_type\": \"markdown\",","   \"metadata\": {},","   \"source\": [","    \"### Preparing inputs for the encoder\\n\",","    \"\\n\",","    \"The encoder needs to be provided with\\n\",","    \"* Columns to be encoded\\n\",","    \"* Exhaustive list of columns that should be generated from one hot encoding\\n\",","    \"\\n\",","    \"Normally, encoders generate the second input on their own. That's actually one of the tasks of one hot encoders. The reason we are tweaking this behavior here (predetermining production needs) is because we need to merge the train and test data, find all unique values in categorical columns and provide these column names to the encoder. If we don't do this, the one hot encoder will only generate hot encoded columns off of train data. This will create issues if your test/validation data has different set of unique values in one of the categorical columns. This will cause the preprocessor to generate a higher/lower number of columns than what the pipeline has been fitted on, hence resulting in errors. Comprende?\"","   ]","  },","  {","   \"cell_type\": \"code\",","   \"execution_count\": 23,","   \"metadata\": {},","   \"outputs\": [","    {","     \"data\": {","      \"text/plain\": [","       \"['REO Resale',\\n\",","       \" 'REO Repossession',\\n\",","       \" 'Land Contract',\\n\",","       \" 'Warranty Deed',\\n\",","       \" \\\"Executor's Deed\\\",\\n\",","       \" \\\"Administrator's Deed\\\",\\n\",","       \" 'Foreclosure',\\n\",","       \" 'Other',\\n\",","       \" 'Bargain and Sale Deed',\\n\",","       \" 'Special Warranty Deed',\\n\",","       \" 'Deed in Lieu of Foreclosure',\\n\",","       \" 'Beneficiary Deed (Buyer ID = \\\"BE\\\")',\\n\",","       \" 'Fiduciary Deed',\\n\",","       \" 'Affidavit',\\n\",","       \" 'Sheriff\\\\'s Deed - Common in New Jersey. 'tax_amount',\\n\",","       \" 'CT',\\n\",","       \" 'NJ']\"","      ]","     },","     \"execution_count\": 23,","     \"metadata\": {},","     \"output_type\": \"execute_result\"","    }","   ],","   \"source\": [","    \"columns_to_encode = categorical_features[categorical_features == True].index.tolist()\\n\",","    \"\\n\",","    \"reindex_hot_encoding = []\\n\",","    \"# Iterating through all the columns in feature set\\n\",","    \"for column in features.columns:\\n\",","    \"    # If the column name is in the columns_to_encode list, append all the unique values of that column\\n\",","    \"    if column in columns_to_encode:\\n\",","    \"        # Ignore the first unique value, we drop it in reindex list instead of using drop=True in get_dummies later\\n\",","    \"        for count, item in enumerate(features[column].unique()):\\n\",","    \"            if count is not 0:\\n\",","    \"                reindex_hot_encoding.append(item)\\n\",","    \"    # If
